Time is Money
Today was the second time John at Angel Nails was late for my appointment -- 15 mins today after the shop owner called him (he was at the bank and not aware of the appt though I saw it written on the schedule book), and 40 mins the time before, again with someone needing to call him. In both instances, I feel a phone call to me explaining that he was running late would of been appropriate as then I could have made a decision to reschedule or cancel. In speaking with the shop owner, she seemed to not really care or even appreciate that I was trying to help bring the disconnect to light so that it could be addressed. < Review>
My boyfriend and I just moved into the Broadcast Apartments and we have loved every minute! Lovely neighbors, clean common areas, responsive management.

We've had a few maintenance requests and they've been really quick and helpful.

The location is unbeatable. We've been jogging through Pan Pacific Park in the mornings (okay, walking) and popping over to The Grove for coffee (okay, ice cream...). But you get the idea -- so far it's been a dream to live here.

We are very grateful to have found this place!</Review>

ATTENTION!!! THIS IS AN HONEST REVIEW OF MY 2+ YEARS HERE!
READ FULLY!!

My last review was November 2018 (scroll down) stating that this is a HORRIBLE place to live if you want to sleep. There is excessive noise from the gym (avoid living above it). Avoid living anywhere near stairs, as this will shake your bedroom when people use it, avoid living here period in my honest opinion unless you are very young, don't work, and definitely don't have kids! Since my last review here are some more issues that management does not care to fully address.

1) Whenever my neighbor uses the washer/dryer my $4000/month "luxury" apartment shakes violently. This building was NOT originally built for washer/dryer in the apartments and the structure doesn't efficiently cancel the noise or 'shaking/vibrating' - there is nothing that can be done at this point because they have installed it in every unit. See below on HOW they installed it too....Expect it to bother you when your neighbor's do their laundry.

2) If you live anywhere the gym, expect to hear noise from people dropping weights, to even general use of the machinery. Like I stated above, the walls and structures are thin, and noise WILL travel through. The gym's hours are from 5am - 12am. Keep in mind and expect to be woken up or annoyed to the fullest extent during those times. They also do not have a courtesy security during times that you really need them. Office hours are 10am -6PM while the gym hours are from 5am to 12am. There is no posted signs of the on-site manager, contact number... nor do they publicize it.

3) DO NOT attempt to work here as a home office - ITS IMPOSSIBLE!!!!

4) The management has strict 'corporate' attitudes that won't bend even the slightest bit for you to accommodate your issues. Everything to them is about them making their quick $$$. Example: I asked them to terminate my lease due to the EXCESSIVE noise but they have refrained from doing so because it would leave them not making any money for a month. While i suffered listening to the high level of noise for 2 years, and was ignored as a resident.

5) Expect fire alarms to go off at all odd times, regardless who pulls the triggers or if it is shared with Erewhon market downstairs, no one at all should ever experience SO MANY false alarms (especially at 2am/3am) These alarms are EAR PIERCING SOUNDS - AN INFANT CAN GO DEAF. In fact, you CANNOT stay in your apartment due to the extreme extreme loud alarm sound. So if it does go off in middle of the night, expect to FLEE your personal space to avoid your ears deafened.

6) To give you an example, of what kind of people they are - they FORCED construction in my unit for 5-6 weeks every morning i was kicked out of my apartment from 8am to 4/5pm because they decided that they want to put washer and dryer units into all apartments. The kicker is that they then subsequently CHARGE you $100+/month for the washer and dryer. There was no way to decline the work if you didn't want the units either. My apartment was dusty, noisy, left a mess more than several times, and really rendered it USELESS between those times. No compensation was given, no rent reduction was given, and no washer/dryer was given to me either unless i PAID them after the disaster construction. Can you imagine what they will do to you when it's time to update the living areas and kitchen areas? I sure as hell don't wish to find out. The LEAST they could have done was give us residents the washer/dryer without charging us.. But again, it's all about their $$..

7) Avoid living across the post office facing the grove drive - you will hear honking, shouting, cars, trucks and endless amounts of noise coming from their employees and method they do business.

8) When moving in ensure that you check your appliances thoroughly to make sure they work properly. I was given a broken refrigerator when i moved in, and my electric bill was double the amount when i moved in. The manager in charge at the time dismissed their responsibility very quickly and was quick to blame me.< /text>

Very unfortunate, don't move here.

[Update:  Just added photos of firefighters attempting to get people out of the same elevator that trapped me for 20 minutes.  Figured I should document these when I see them come to rescue people trapped in the same elevator over and over.  This is at least the third time I've seen firefighters come for this elevator.]

So many residents here don't even bother leaving their apartments because of how many false alarms there have been.  And why have they happened, where here's the running list of reasons I've gotten from management:
Multiple times it was the vendor's fault for apparently "tripping" the fire alarm during some sheet rock installations or something.
A couple of times it apparently could have been a prank, but don't worry, they ostensibly found out who it was and stopped that.
And MOSTLY it has been due to the system just being riddled with malfunctions.

The false alarms have gone off at 4AM, at 6AM, at 11PM; it's been pretty time-indiscriminate.  Try getting back to sleep after waking up to a 4AM fire alarm and having to make your way down 6 flights of stairs (I'm on the top floor).

It's downright negligent, and is past the point of dangerous.

Next, the elevators.

Well, they are frequently malfunctioning and being taken offline.  It would seem that they would get them serviced properly, once, but they've gone down far more frequently than any other building I've ever been in. That only happened to me once, but the other night, fire engines showed up because it happened to someone else apparently.

Okay fine, I get it, stuff needs to be maintained on the roof. I'm fairly certain this phrase was written in hopes that it would distract all the current residents for the very inconvenient times that lie ahead.  We were informed that construction crews would be in and out of the apartments for 3 weeks.  Starting on the first day, while I was in the shower, I received a knock on my door.  Not my apartment door, but my bedroom door.  I turned off the shower to tell them I needed a second to put some clothes on.  This happened two more times as the crew seemingly likes to come in no matter what.  Pretty inconvenient.

About mid week I received an email from Cherokii asking us, "if you have made a decision on whether you would like the new washer and dryer amenity added to your home. This will add $100 per month to your lease and the convenience of not having to travel to a separate area with your laundry."  This was just a promotional price, that will go up once the construction is finished(if it's ever finished.)  I stated, in my response, how ridiculous it is to be asking current residents to pay even more than we pay now for these "luxury" apartments, and that I would like the washer and dryer installed for a fair price of $0 a month.  Cherokii said no, obviously.  I never expected anything else.

The next week, I came home to my room completely uprooted.  The construction crew is supposed to put everything they've moved, back to where they found it when they are done for the day.  My nightstand, light fixtures, and other electronics were left on the complete other side of the room.  I took a picture of this and sent it to Cherokii on 8/20, and have still not received a response.  This is just a small sample size of the complete lack of care that the management team has for this property. They also leave the doors open while they work and after they leave so we have a bunch of bugs around our apartment.

We also received a letter stating that construction is going to be extended for another 2 weeks.  So 5 weeks total of them being in your apartment from 8:00 am - 6 pm.  Can't imagine what you would do if you worked from home or had a pet.

Security: The fab entry from the garage to the elevator is consistently broken.  You can see the footmarks of people breaking into it.  They paint it over once a month to cover it up.  Usually, that elevator is broken or being used by the construction team.  When that is happening you have to use the stairs, but sometimes the door to the garage from the stairs is locked from the inside, so there's literally no way into the garage save walking all the way out of the building and in from the front.  Convenient.

Management:  Rude.  Unhelpful.  Dismissive.

AirBnB:  Strictly forbidden...Unless you want to do it.  There have been countless amounts of airbnb'ers coming in and out of the building.  I think management is trying to stop this, but clearly, it's not working.

How long are these reviews allowed to be?  I could go forever.  I'll let my roommate tell you about the massive bugs in his review.</Review>

< Text>
Very disappointed in the leasing process at Broadcast Center apartments. Saw a posting for a 1 bedroom apartment available August 18 advertised on Apartment Search. We had already been in contact with Barry at Broadcast Center regarding other apartments available. We requested they send us quotes for this apartment and another apartment available August 15th.They did. We decided to move forward with the August 18th apartment since this was less expensive. We filled out the entire leasing application and paid $1,000 holding deposit and $87 application fee. After we were finished and I was mentally moving in...we received an email saying the apartment was all set... For a Jan 1 move in date. Say what?!

We contacted them... Surely just a mistake in the system. No, when we finally got a response from Barry we were told he talked to "corporate" and that someone else leased the apartment at the exact same time we filled out our application. Really? Someone leased an apartment from August 18- jan 1? That's 4.5 months. The minimum lease they offer is 6 months. Now, we were told, the only apartment available August was $600 more than previous. Thanks but no thanks. Regardless  of whether or not we can afford this, I will NEVER give Broadcast Center or any other companies that use bait and switch tactics a dime. Interestingly, an apartment the same size and same price was listed on Apartment Search the next day. Be on guard for ghost listings by this company! Also, it took almost TWO MONTHS to get our money back. We had to dispute it with our credit card company and jump through lots of hoops to get our $$. And they asked if they could send us a check instead of returning it to our credit card!

Drop-off at this place was ok, which is the reason I‚Äôm giving it two stars, rather than one. We returned from our trip from Mexico around 10pm. It was 58 degrees outside...cold considering we had just returned from Puerto Vallarta and were only wearing shorts and t-shirts. They told us they were leaving right immediately to pick us up. After freezing for 20 minutes we called them back to find out where they were. They told us that they were nearby and to continue waiting. After 40 minutes of shivering, we called them to inform them that we had decided to take a cab to their lot because we couldn‚Äôt wait in the cold any longer. However, they wouldn't answer their phone. In fact, their voicemail wasn‚Äôt even "set up" so we couldn‚Äôt leave a message. We tried numerous times calling, but no answer. So, we jumped in the cab and drove to their lot. When we arrived, their gate was closed, locked, and their office (trailer) was dark. We tried calling all three numbers posted on their gate. Same thing, no answer. We honked the horn of the cab several times, flashed the bright lights through their gate, and even yelled to see if anyone was there. Nothing! After roughly another 15 minutes, the driver showed up and told us that he couldn't find us at CBX...even though we stood exactly where he told us to (right in front of the CBX sign near the driveway entrance...there's only one). <Text>Long wait just for cookies, but we wanted to see what the hype was all about! The smell of sugar permeated through our masks when we finally got in the door. Quick ordering when you know what you want. I mean, if you're waiting 20/30 minutes in line, you would think everyone would already know what they want by the time they approach the counter, right? Wrong. That's what holds up the line! LOL. The cookies smelled great, the kitchen was super busy! Cleanliness was a bit lacking if you ask me, refrigerator handles stayed dirty, kitchen staff all over the place with flour, eggs, oil, the boxes that the customers receive their cookies in are riddled with icing...messy, but the constant demand must make it tough to keep up? We ordered the 12 pack party box because why not? Cookies were very inconsistent as far as size, decorations/icing and amount of chocolate chips. A little disappointing to get a big chocolate chip cookie and your first few bites have ZERO chips. Errrggg. If it didn't taste like yummy butter cookies on it's own, I would have called to complain. My 2 dirt cake cookies were very dissimilar too, it was very evident that someone was cutting corners with the icing...wish I noticed before I left the store. Will I go back? Possibly...just to try some of the new flavors (that's the attraction I guess...always in search for the new stuff?) It's just sad to see that the fast paced work in the store makes employees serve inferior products for the prices you pay and the time you spend in line. Make sure you check the quality of your cookies before you leave!</Text></record></dataset><record>

Veg momos tasted pretty good, but there was oil flowing out of it if you break it. Are momos not supposed to be filled with steamed veggies, or stir fry at the max? It was more than deep friend - it just had oil flowing.

We ordered catering from Namastee Nepal and the whole company loved it. They said the food was delicious and interesting. We ordered the lollipops, chow mein, vegetarian rolls, white rice and vegetable fried rice. The trays were scrapped clean and people took hone leftovers. Thank you Namastee Nepal!
